Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "107", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/4432669301440408838/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "2801759492367904670", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2012-09-07T22:46:00+05:30", "updated": "2016-11-29T21:57:21+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxNDgwNDM2ODQxOTAwCm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2012/09/ums-operations-on-chemical-tankers-capt_7.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/2801759492367904670", "title": "UMS OPERATIONS ON CHEMICAL TANKERS - CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL  ", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\">\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-hDqyg9UEHv8/UEoppEXF2nI/AAAAAAAARG0/pdTBQXF7TE0/s1600/AAA.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-hDqyg9UEHv8/UEoppEXF2nI/AAAAAAAARG0/pdTBQXF7TE0/s1600/AAA.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\"><b>UMS OPERATIONS ON\nCHEMICAL TANKERS - CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL&nbsp;&nbsp;</b></span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;\n<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">AUTOMATION AT SEA IS\nNOT SAFE, &nbsp;IF PROPER PROCEDURES ARE NOT FOLLOWED. THESE PROCEDURES MUST BE IN\nWRITING.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">UMS operations are\nprohibited on chemical tankers , without the prior authorisation of the Master.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">There must be close\nliason between bridge and ECR when a change over takes place. The bridge\nwatchkeeper must be informed on start and finish of UMS operations and he must\nrecord the relevant times in the Deck Log Book.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">E/R doors must not be\nlocked.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">If a fire alarm gets\nactivated during UMS period, all personnel must report to their fire station.\nEntry to engine room can be decided only by chief engineer after consultation\nwith master.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Prior to commencing UMS\noperations the correct functioning of the Duty Engineer call out system must be\nverified. The Chief Engineer and Duty Engineer cabin alarm and the bridge alarm\nmust be functioning correctly prior to commencing UMS operations.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Upon commencement of\nUMS operations an announcement is to be made on the public address system\ninforming all ship's personnel that the engine room is unmanned and that entry\nis forbidden without the permission of or under instruction from the Chief\nEngineer, Second Engineer, Master or Duty Engineer. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Should this not be\npossible other means must be adopted to ensure that all ship's personnel are\naware that the engine room is operating in an unmanned condition. Suitable\nnotices must be prominently displayed in way of the doors indicating that the\nengine room is unmanned and that unauthorised entry is forbidden<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">If an activated\nmachinery alarm is not acknowledged by the duty engineer, the engineers call\nalarm in the accommodation will be triggered after a reasonable set time delay.\nThe activation of such a call&nbsp; alarm must\nbe verified and logged in the UMS log book.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The engine room must be\nvisited by duty engineer for an inspection round during the UMS period. This\nshould normally occur between 2200 to 2400 hrs.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Max UMS period between\n2 rounds is 8 hours.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Meal break maximum 60\nminutes.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Duty engineer must\nchange machinery operation to manned condition before entry of crew.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Duty engineer cannot\nenter the UMS engine room without alerting the bridge watchkeeper. This alert\nand the subsequent ( every 15 minute) alert should be recorded in the bridge\nlog book. A radio linked personnel accident alarm may be used in lieu of this\n15 minute alert.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">All alarms during the\nUMS period must be recorded in the UMS log book which should be sighted by\nchief engineer daily.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Necessary written\nsafety precautions should be clearly displayed at all entrances to unmanned\nmachinery spaces. Warning should also be given that machinery is likely to\nstart automatically like compressor.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">All UMS machinery\nspaces should always be adequately illuminated.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">When machinery is on\nbridge control, the bridge must be advised when a change in machinery setting\nis contemplated by the engine room staff, and before changing machinery to\nengine room control. Same will be logged.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Ships must not be\noperated in UMS mode without an appropriate valid endorsement on the ship's\nCertificate of Class.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Sensors and Alarms must\nbe under a PLANNED MAINTENENCE SCHEME.&nbsp;\nThis means sensors must be calibrated and alarms tested.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">UMS is prohibited if---<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">--The fire/smoke\ndetection system is inoperative<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">--The ship is\nmanoevering is congested waters<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">--Tank cleaning\noperations are in progress<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">--When the ship is\ncarrying heated cargo and is not equipped with a chemical detection&nbsp; alarm in the heating coil return which will\nactivate the UMS alarm.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">--Speed adjustments may\nbe made to combat weather<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">--Critical alarms are\ninoperative. Example\u2014high level alarms, jockey pump failure alarm etc<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">--Bridge control system\nor emergency stop system is inoperative<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">--Remote starting of\nelectric fire pump is inoperative<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">--Bridge , chief\nengineer cabin, duty engineer cabin UMS alarms ( visual/ audible ) are\ninoperative. The activation of the engineer\u2019s alarm on non-acceptance of a UMS\nalarm is not available<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">--During cargo and\nballast transfer operations.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">--Nitrogen generator is\nin operation.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">--Critical alarms are\ninoperative. These are considered to be alarms or trips that affect equipment\nessential to the safe navigation and operation of the ship and machinery plant.\nThis includes the link between the machinery alarm system and the engineers call\nout alarm. It also includes items that could have an environmental effect such\nas fuel oil and bilge water tank high level alarms etc.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">--Any item of equipment\nis inoperative that is essential to the safe navigation of the ship, safe\noperation of the machinery/ship or is a requirement of class for UMS operation.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">--Any control system\nthat affects equipment essential to the safe navigation and operation of the\nship and machinery plant is inoperative<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">--Should a UMS alarm\nremain unaccepted longer than the time at which the engineer's alarm should\nhave been activated, the bridge watchkeeper must call the Chief Engineer and\ninform him of the situation.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; font-size: large;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif; font-size: large;\">A few years back, you\nwrote a letter to Jenab Mohammad Hamid Ansari, then Chairman, National\nCommission for Minorities, where you complained of harassment of nuns and\nChristian workers at bus stops and rail stations in Tirupati government-owned\nareas and objecting to a request to have the Constitutionality of the Seven\nTirumala Hills being made out of bounds to Christians.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif; Its most insidious and dangerous arm is urban Naxalism.<br />\n<br />\nThe GURU of Fourth Generation Warfare, William Lind observes that \u201cif nation-states are going to survive, people in power must earn and keep the trust of the governed\u201d..<br />\n<br />\nThis fourth generation war is complex and long-term. It is decentralised, small in size and lacks hierarchy.<br />\n<br />\nThe strategy is to make a direct attack on the enemy\u2019s (in this case, the Indian state) culture, including genocidal acts against civilians and wage a highly sophisticated psychological and cultural warfare, especially through media manipulation and lawfare.<br />\n<br />\nAll available pressures are used \u2014 political, economic, social and military. For this purpose, legal professionals are required, media professionals are required, creative people, varied intellectuals and academicians are required, and civil society leaders are required, especially those who are connected with NGOs. It begins with low-intensity conflicts where all the actors attack from different platforms.<br />\n<br />\nIn 2004, the Communist Party of India (Marxist\u2013Leninist) People\u2019s War, usually called People\u2019s War Group, merged with the Maoist Communist Centre of India and formed the Communist Party of India (Maoist), pledging to the ideology of Marxism-Leninism-Maoism. The party became a member of the Coordination Committee of Maoist Parties and Organisations of South Asia.<br />\n<br />\nThis new entity drafted a blueprint for their urban movement/activities. It is believed that Kobad Ghandy, who was arrested in September 2009 in New Delhi, played a major role in the preparation of this urban perspective plan.<br />\n<br />\nThe document admits that the enemy is very strong in urban areas and therefore should never be engaged with until the conditions are favourable. And to make them favourable, it suggests the exploring and opening of opportunities, and organising people through front organisations.<br />\n<br />\nTarget the \u201cvulnerable group\u201d of minorities, women, Dalits, labourers and students through influencers who work undercover for a long time and accumulate strength. The document stresses on uniting industrial proletariats and students, and using them as vanguards who can play a direct role in revolution.<br />\n<br />\nThe city becomes the money source, shelter for cadre as transit points, source of weaponry and legal protection, medical aid, media attention and intelligentsia network.<br />\n<br />\nThe stronger the movement becomes in urban areas, the more likely it is to contribute to the agrarian revolution, in terms of providing leaders, men and material to the people\u2019s war.<br />\n<br />\nThe majority of the people in Maoist-affected areas and even their supporters and cadres have little to do with Maoism at the ideological level. They are only alienated and angry people with a sense of injustice, oppression and indignity.<br />\n<br />\nMaoists cleverly exploit this sentiment to their advantage \u2014 caste conflicts in Bihar, resentment against landlords in Andhra Pradesh, discontent against forest laws in tribal areas, unemployment amongst youth, radicalism among Muslims are all given the prescription of capture of power through the gun.<br />\n<br />\nWhile local grievances need to be effectively addressed through improved governance and ruthless accountability, there is an urgent need for creating mass awareness of the ultimate designs and consequences of what the extremists stand for.<br />\n<br />\nThe forest-based rebellion survives mostly on what Maoist ideologue Varavara Rao calls the \u201cmovement in urban areas\u201d. The network is spread across five states: Tamil Nadu, Andhra, Madhya Pradesh, Chhattisgarh and Odisha.<br />\n<br />\nIn the cities, an invisible naxal-intelligentsia-media-academia-NGO-activist nexus works as strategic fortification with the ultimate aim of taking over the Indian state to achieve Maoist rule. , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">After\nGandhi's assassination Savarkar's home in Mumbai was stoned by angry Hindu mobs.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Badge's testimony was rejected\nby the British (on recommendation of Jews Rothschild ), as lacking credibility and Veer\nVinayak Savarkar was released.. &nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><b>Rothschilds and their stooge Winston Churcill would NOT harm anybody who supports Jews and Israel.&nbsp;</b><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><i><span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Only after the death of\nNehru, the Congress government, under Prime Minister Shastri, started to pay\nVeer Savarkar a monthly pension.&nbsp; On Feb\n26th 1966, Veer Vinayak Savarkar renounced medicines, food and water leading to\nhis own death on February 26, 1966.&nbsp;</span></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><i><span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><i><span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Not a single minister from the Maharashtra\nCabinet showed up in the cremation ground to pay homage to Savarkar. In New\nDelhi, the Speaker of the Parliament turned down a request that it pay homage\nto Savarkar.&nbsp; PM Morajee Desai and\nCongress Home minister YB Chawan refused to visit the cell of Veer Savarkar\nwhen they went to Cellular jail.<o:p></o:p></span></i></span><br />\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><i><span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-5FYlnEUObhk/UETpeQPh0TI/AAAAAAAAQoM/dArBohy9Jfo/s1600/imagesnbccc.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-5FYlnEUObhk/UETpeQPh0TI/AAAAAAAAQoM/dArBohy9Jfo/s1600/imagesnbccc.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"background-color: yellow; color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i>After the unveiling of\nportrait of Veer Savarkar in the Indian Parliament in February 2003 there was a\nlot of mudslinging against him in the English newspapers. The main accusation\nwas that Veer Savarkar apologised for his deeds to seek release from jail in\nAndaman Islands. </i><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">OK, now-- I must stop digressing in this manner--&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"background-color: yellow; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow; line-height: 150%;\">I must get\nback to my subject matter , Ganesh Baburao Savarkar-- the elder brother of Veer\nVinayak Sarvarkar. This man went through the same torture as his younger\nbrother, but he was made of steel and never ever would agree to a dishonourable clemency\nplea- even if he was fried in boiling oil.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Ganesh Babarao\nSavarkar's<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"> life story make terrific reading.&nbsp;\nThis is the meaning of love for the motherland and a shining&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 24px;\">example</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;of\nindefatigable human spirit.&nbsp; His story\nmust be available in every Military Establishment in India. &nbsp;Our Indian jawans must know about him. --NOT\n</span>Rahul<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"> Gandhi or Dig </span>Vijay<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"> Singh or </span>Ambika Soni<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"> or </span>Kapil Sibal<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">..<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Ganesh Savarkar\u2019s pro-active\nresistance against the British colonial government in India, caused him to be\ntransported for life to Cellular jail.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">For this unfair deportation, the then collector of\nNasik, Jackson was assassinated by Anant Laxman Kanhere, another unsung\nfreedom fighter, &nbsp;in direct retaliation.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-vMG9hG6R4UU/UETnYHwi9dI/AAAAAAAAQnU/MCudfwT6Iiw/s1600/hutatma+anant+laxman+kanhere.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-vMG9hG6R4UU/UETnYHwi9dI/AAAAAAAAQnU/MCudfwT6Iiw/s320/hutatma+anant+laxman+kanhere.JPG\" width=\"213\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Kanhere, on 21 December\n1909, shot Jackson, the Collector of Nashik of British India. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Nashik was a hub of\nanti-invader activities under a revolutionary organization Abhinav Bharat\nSociety founded by Ganseh Babarao Savarkar .. They held secret meetings and planned organized resistance<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Jackson, the British\nCollector of Nasik, was aware of these activities.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Jackson started mixing with local people. Unlike other British officers, he created an image of himself as a Indian people\nfriendly officer. He gave unsolicited propaganda that he was a Vedic literate Brahmin in his\nprevious life and that was why he felt so much fatherly affection towards the Indian people.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Jackson used to talk to people in Marathi and had some knowledge of Sanskrit. &nbsp;In reality,\nhis intentions were to make the people feel that they are good and safe in slavery\nand hence had to to squeal on any anti-British activities.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Shouting the slogan of\n'Vande Mataram' written by Bankim Chandra Chattopadhyay in 1882 was enough\nreason to be imprisoned for sedition.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">On 20 July 1905, Lord\nCurzon announced the partition of Bengal. This raised a storm of protest\nthroughout the country.&nbsp; Babarao Ganesh\norganized a spate of patriotic lectures in Nashik.The atmosphere in Nashik\nbecame charged with patriotic fervour. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The annual Dassara\nprocession organized by the Mitramel was returning from the Kalika Mandir. &nbsp;Babarao and other members raised loud joyful slogans of Vande Mataram.&nbsp; On the pretext that these slogans disturbed the\nBritish residents, a British police officer, gave a hard blow on Babarao\u2019s head with his baton.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Enraged,\nBabarao ( who had balls ) leapt upon him and caught him by his throat and\nthrashed him soundly.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Ganesh Babarao Savarkar was arrested promptly. &nbsp;All this was a\ntrap, and he fell into it neatly. The British just wanted him out of Nasik.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The arrested\nrevolutionaries were tried before the First Class Magistrate of Malegaon\ndivision, W. Plunkett. It dragged on for one year and became famous throughout\nMaharashtra as the Vande Mataram trial. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Jackson was\ninstrumental in getting Babarao indicted for writing a 16 page song book of\nKavi Govind. &nbsp;He had also planted some incriminating \"bomb making\nmanuals\" in his house at Tulsi Vrindavan. &nbsp;The verdict was a foregone\nconclusion. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">As proof, that he was a terrorist, the British government submitted&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 24px;\">frivolously</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp; in court that Babarao had worn his dhoti in a particular fashion and was also\nwearing the langot (small inner loin garment) in a peculiar manner!<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Justice BC Kennedy\npronounced the judgement on 08 June 1909. He grandly ruled: \u201cThe Penal Code has\ngiven me very little leeway to decide the quantum of the punishment. Under\nsection 121, I sentence Ganesh Damodar Savarkar to Transportation for Life or\nkaala pani ( lit: black waters; incarceration in the black hole of the\nAndamans) and order forfeiture of his entire property and - \u201cUnder section\n124A, I sentence him to two years\u2019 rigorous imprisonment. This sentence has to\nbe served simultaneously with the sentence given under section 121.\u201d&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Babarao\nwas now made to don the prisoner\u2019s garb and the yellow cap meant for the Kaala Pani\nprisoners.<o:p></o:p></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-8DR-hta8nr8/UETrIn0y_lI/AAAAAAAAQpE/Rf0eiE1kb9Y/s1600/imagesasd.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-8DR-hta8nr8/UETrIn0y_lI/AAAAAAAAQpE/Rf0eiE1kb9Y/s1600/imagesasd.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">On 09 June 1909, a\ntelegram was sent from Nashik to London informing the news of Babarao\u2019s overseas transportation. &nbsp;The news created a wave of seething anger among the Indian\nrevolutionaries in London. &nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red;\"><br /></span></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">On 01 July 1909,&nbsp;\na patriot <b style=\"background-color: yellow;\">Madanlal Dhingra </b>assassinated Curzon Wylie at a public meeting\nin London. <o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">How many of you know of\nan Indian by the name of Dhingra?&nbsp; All you\nknow is Sonia Gandhi, Ambika Soni, Anand Sharma , Kapil Sibal , BR Ambedkar, Teesta Setalvad etc , right?</span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><i><span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">05 July 1909, a meeting\nwas held in Caxton Hall to condemn Madan Lal Dhingra. Aga Khan was in the\nChair. The motion was proposed by Bhavanagari and seconded by Amir Ali. &nbsp;Aga\nKhan put the motion to vote.&nbsp;</span></i></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><i><span style=\"color: blue;\"><br /></span></i></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><i><span style=\"color: blue;\">After seeing many raised hands, he declared that the\nmotion was passed unanimously. Savarkar stood up and cried, \" No, not\nunanimously. There are opponents of the motion as well. Take down my name, it is Vinayak\nDamodar Savarkar. &nbsp;I oppose this motion.\u201d&nbsp;</span></i></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><i><span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">A Eurasian named Palmer hit Veer\nSavarkar near his eye making him bleed profusely .&nbsp; Savarkar said, \"I still oppose the\nmotion.\"&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></i></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><i><span style=\"color: blue;\"><br /></span></i></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><i><span style=\"color: blue;\">M P T Acharya, a friend of\nSavarkar then hammered Palmer with a stick. &nbsp;Surendranath Banerjee , a known British stooge , ( who would be knighted later ) expressed his fake anger. He said \" Vinayak Savarkar has a right to have his say. It is\noutrageous to attack him.\u201d &nbsp;</span></i></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><i><span style=\"color: blue;\"><br /></span></i></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><i><span style=\"color: blue;\">Vinayak Savarkar wanted to Dhingra's ashes to be\nrespectfully collected and sent to India for immersion in Indian rivers .</span></i></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Several members\nof Secretary Morley's Council favoured life imprisonment rather than the death\nsentence for Dhingra. They feared that his martyrdom would ignite further acts\nof retribution.&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red;\"><br /></span></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">Dhingra's valour infuriated King Emperor Edward VII. &nbsp;In a\nletter dated 17 August 1909, he wrote to Morley that Indians be barred from\ncoming to England without valid reason. Such students learn treason while in\nEngland and incite others back home, he fumed.</span></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-9LSCkJMOsIs/UETnwva1QSI/AAAAAAAAQnc/_zHRLAAzgYY/s1600/dhingra.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-9LSCkJMOsIs/UETnwva1QSI/AAAAAAAAQnc/_zHRLAAzgYY/s1600/dhingra.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">In his memoirs, Wilfrid Scawen\nBlunt, the British poet and writer who also served in the Diplomatic Service\nwrites (entry dated 24 July 1909) writes, \"No Christian martyr ever faced\nhis judges more fearlessly or with greater dignity...if India could produce\nfive hundred such sons, as resolute without fear, she would achieve her freedom\".&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">It\nwas recorded in medical evidence at the trial, that, when arrested, Dhingra's\npulse beat no quicker than normal, nor from first to last, has he shown any\nsign of weakening.\" &nbsp; False rumors were spread by the British that he had Bhang and hence his pulse was strong and steady.&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red;\"><br /></span></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">On the day of Dhingra's martyrdom, leaflets entitled\n'Ireland Honours Dhingra' were distributed and pasted on walls in Ireland.&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Back home in India, the Deputy Superintendent\nof Police Guyder threw the bait to Babarao \u201cWe have arrested your two brothers.\nTell me the names of revolutionaries and their addresses in Nashik. If you\nprovide this information, we will release you and your brothers..We will ensure\nyour protection after your release and provide a monthly pension to you. Do not\nbe afraid.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">It was unthinkable for\nBabarao to expose his colleagues for selfish reasons.&nbsp; Seeing Babarao smiling , Guyder&nbsp; threatened Babarao. Guyder cried \u201c If you do NOT give me a list and full information, be assured that you will get a second Transportation \u201c<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Babarao laughed and said \u201cThe question of a second transportation would arise, only if I survive the\nfirst one, right? . &nbsp;So why bother?&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Guyder was furious \u201c I\nunderstand your clever witticisms. Remember, the name is Guyder. I have seen\nseveral patriots like you and have brought them to heel with whiplashes. Will\nyou open your mouth or not? Do you see what I have with me?\u201d&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">And he showed the\nelectric shock device with wires. The mere sight of these electric wires was enough\nto make the most hardened criminals soil their pants .&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Guyder asked thrice and\ngave shocks after every negative answer he got&nbsp;\n. All three times his body flexed like a bent bow in&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 24px;\">excruciating</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;pain , but\nnot a word escaped from Babarao\u2019s lips.&nbsp;\nGuyder had to accept defeat. &nbsp;As Babarao turned to limp back to his cell,\nGuyder could not but help exclaim, \u201cBrave bloody fella!\u201d<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The residents of Nashik\nhad immense respect for Babarao. To demoralize them, the British paraded\nBabarao in fetters. &nbsp;Babarao, the lion, was paraded in disgrace through the\nstreets of Nashik with his hands and feet in handcuffs and fetters, the yellow\ncap serving a dire warning and striking terror in the hearts of all onlookers.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">For melodramatic and sarcastic effect they\nmade him carry a bundle of his clothes, plate and water pot balanced\nprecariously on his back. &nbsp;Smirking armed guards walked in front and behind him. &nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Babarao\nbraved this humiliation with fortitude. &nbsp;People in tears lined up on both sides\nof the street to have his last darshan, before was shipped off.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Ganesh Damodar Savarkar\nwas sentenced to life imprisonment and deportation, overseas at Andamans. He\nwas transported to Andamans on the ship MV.Maharaja. This ship would make nine\ntrips to the Andamans in a year and transport prisoners from Madras ,\nCalcutta&nbsp; and Rangoon to the Andamans.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">In\nthe underbelly of this ship was a long and narrow cage. Prisoners would be\npacked like sardines in this cage and chained..The stench in the ship's ill ventilated compartment was unbearable.<o:p></o:p></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-rusRt_ix-9U/UETpWSSEcbI/AAAAAAAAQoE/jnP9IVyPVM0/s1600/imagesngfss.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"240\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-rusRt_ix-9U/UETpWSSEcbI/AAAAAAAAQoE/jnP9IVyPVM0/s320/imagesngfss.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">I would suggest to every patriotic Indian , to visit this jail, like how Muslims have to go to Mecca. &nbsp;Only then you will understand why you and your children are free and happy today. &nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><b>I have seen this Cellular jail at Port Blair, myself.</b></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">The Cellular Jail was completed in 1906 and\nthe number of prisoners it housed was as high as 14086 . Like an predator octopus having\neight arms to catch its prey, the Cellular Jail had seven protruding arms or\nwings from the central watchtower.The Jail was constructed with seven wings,\nspreading out like a seven-petal flower. In its centre it had a tower with a\nturret.&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-M6OO8uxGutw/UETqsSD345I/AAAAAAAAQo0/G5SIpdGz8Zc/s1600/imagesrgvxxx.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"262\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-M6OO8uxGutw/UETqsSD345I/AAAAAAAAQo0/G5SIpdGz8Zc/s400/imagesrgvxxx.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Connected to this were the three storey high seven wings with 698\nisolated cells. That is why it was called the Cellular Jail. Each wing had\nthree floors with 698 cells. Each cell measured 4.1 by 1.9 metres, just enough\nfor one convict. These small cells gave the Cellular Jail its name. &nbsp;All the\nseven wings of the Cellular Jail had a meeting point at the central watchtower\nfor entry and exit.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Each cell had separate iron bolts and locking devices\noutside, beyond the reach of the prisoner\u2019s hand. Though there was no chance of\nan escape, there was constant vigil by 21 wardens; seven on each floor facing\ntheir respective wings.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">There were sentries in the central watchtower. To\nminimize the chances of communication between the convicts and to isolate them\nfrom each other, the construction of the Cellular Jail was made such that the\nfront portion of each wing faced the back side of the other wing at a\nsufficient distance.</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-xGNF_YtIri8/UETqEFvQixI/AAAAAAAAQok/wqcY4kt4FCU/s1600/imageskrfdaxxvb.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"299\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-xGNF_YtIri8/UETqEFvQixI/AAAAAAAAQok/wqcY4kt4FCU/s400/imageskrfdaxxvb.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">There were no dormitories in the Cellular Jail. On arrival\nin th cellular Jail, convicts would be placed in solitary confinement for six\nmonths. This helped to tone down their vigour and vitality and demoralize them.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Thus the Cellular Jail was a prison within a prison!<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">In March 1868, 238\nprisoners tried to escape from Cellular jail. &nbsp;By April they were all caught. &nbsp;One committed suicide and of the remainder Superintendent Walker ordered 87 to\nbe hanged. &nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">There was a solitary first strike , before the mass second strike under the leadership of Babarao.&nbsp;\nMahavir Singh, an associate of Bhagat Singh (Lahore conspiracy case) protested\nthe inhuman treatment meted to the prisoners and sat in hunger strike.&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">He was\nforce fed milk which went into his lungs and he died. He was tied to a stone\nand thrown in the sea.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">The Empire of Japan\ninvaded the Andaman islands in 1942 and drove the British out. The Cellular\nJail then became home to British prisoners. During this period, </span>Subhas<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"> Chandra\nBose also visited the islands. Two out of the seven wings of the Jail were\ndemolished during the Japanese regime. In 1945, the British resumed control\nwith the end of World War II. &nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Another two wings of the jail were demolished\nafter India achieved independence, with Nehru\u2019s&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 24px;\">connivance</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">.&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">This led\nto protests from several former prisoners and political leaders who saw it as a\nway of erasing the tangible evidence of their persecution. &nbsp;The remaining three\nwings and the central tower were therefore converted into a National Memorial\nin 1969. &nbsp; The centenary of the jail's\ncompletion was marked on 10 March 2006. &nbsp;Many erstwhile prisoners were felicitated\non this occasion by the Government of India. They were taken in SCI ships as passengers.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Babarao would be at\nAndamans like a living corpse in a tiny cell&nbsp;\nfor the next 25 years-- as per the British sentence.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The infamous Irish\njailor Barrie, the terror of the Cellular Jail was apprised of the arrival of\nBabarao Ganesh , to give him special treatment. &nbsp;He sought out Ganesh and loudly\nexplained to him the rules and regulations of the Cellular Jail. \u201cIf you break\nrules, remember you will have to deal with me\u201d he threatened.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">He spent most of his\ntime in doing CHAKKI PEESING or extracting oil from coconuts--hard labour\nthroughout the day. The prisoner would be yoked like a bullock to the metal bar\nand made to push it around in a circle so that dried coconut pieces kept in a central receptacle would get crushed and oil would drip<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">After he did his part\nof chakki peesing, he would be handcuffed to a hook on the wall at his height.\nThe cook was a Muslim, and a British informer, who would put light doses of\nKerosene in the food, giving him bloody stools with mucous, and making his\ndehydrated and weak. &nbsp;When Babarao Ganesh passed stools while hanging on his\nwrists, the jailer would beat him up for dirtying the place.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The other political\nprisoners, all knew the worth of Ganesh Savarkar. They tried their best to make\nhim comfortable. They would weave bundles of the coarse coconut husk and throw it\ntowards Babarao so as to lighten his burden, on weaving day. &nbsp;In helping Babarao, the other\nprisoners were risking terrible torture, and beatings by the warden . Knowing\nthis Babarao would refuse help from his fellow prisoners.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Jackson tortured Vaman\nSakharam Khare, a well-known lawyer, for pleading for Ganesh and Khare lost his\nmental balance when his property was confiscated by Jackson and sent to\njail.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">He got he due from </span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><b style=\"background-color: yellow;\">Anant Laxman\nKanhere.</b><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">K</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">anhere , a 19 year old\nstudent took a pistol and emptied it on Jackson on the night of 21\nDecember, 1909 at the Vijayanand Theatre, Nashik. In his declaration, Kanhere\nsaid, \u201cI have just done my duty. Jackson was instrumental in the deportation of Ganesh\nBaburao Savarkar\"<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Kanhere\u2019s dignity and\ncourage in the face of certain death moved even the sentencing judge Justice\nHeeton to exclaim, \u201cWhat a pity that I have to send such a handsome and\ncourageous youth to the gallows.\u201d<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Babarao was married at\nthe age of 13 to \u201cYesuvahini\u201d. &nbsp;He was a yogi and used to practise austerities\nsuch as surviving on ghee and water only a full month, and remaining awake for\nlong times without sleeping, to expand his consciousness.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">There is no coming to\nconsciousness without pain and penance.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Yesuvahini used to live\nin the upper storey of the Datar family house in Nashik. The police came and\nconfiscated the household items including her Puja items.\u2014they exactly knew what they\nwere doing. .It was Yesuvahini\u2019s habit not to touch food or water without\nperforming puja and watering the tulsi plant.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Tears streaming from here eyes, she went to the local cemetery\nand lay down. She was childless and young. Her husband Babarao Ganesh Savarkar\nwas transported to Kaala Pani for life.&nbsp;\nAfter noon, a kind woman gave her some puja vessels and Yesuvahini\nreturned ,performed her daily rituals and ate food. .</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-hVZCFsEsR7I/UETodIg5Y-I/AAAAAAAAQn0/g0Z4ijl5C_U/s1600/downloadccde.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-hVZCFsEsR7I/UETodIg5Y-I/AAAAAAAAQn0/g0Z4ijl5C_U/s320/downloadccde.jpg\" width=\"286\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The Datars looked after\nYesuvahini till her death. &nbsp;Madame Cama used to send Rs 30 every month, which Yesuvahini gave to Narayanrao. &nbsp;Of this, Baburao\u2019s youngest brother Narayanrao would spend\nRs. 15 on his own education and Rs.15 would be given for Yesuvahini\u2019s upkeep.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Meanhile Narayanrao was\narrested on the false charges of throwing a bomb on the viceroy Minto .\nThis&nbsp; arrest took away Yesuvahini\u2019s last moral support. &nbsp;For this childless woman, Narayanrao was like her own son . &nbsp;Narayanrao was\nreleased by the British on 18 December 1909.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Narayanrao was arrested\nagain on the midnight of 23 December. &nbsp;He was mercilessly tortured. &nbsp;In London,\nthe other brother Vinayak Tatyarao Savarkar was arrested for his alleged role\nin the Nashik conspiracy &nbsp;(to kill Jackson ). &nbsp;On 24 December 1910, Vinayak Savarkar was\nsentenced to transportation for life at Cellular jail Andamans Islands , and Narayanrao was\nsentenced to six months rigorous imprisonment.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Virtually every\npatriotic young man in Nashik was placed in handcuffs. &nbsp;A reign of terror was\nlet loose in Nashik. &nbsp;People for their own survival started shunning any one was\nlinked directly or indirectly to revolutionary activities. &nbsp;&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">People now turned their backs on Yesuvahini,\nas the police were watching every inch of her movements. The poet Govind had composed a moving poem specially\nfor Yesuvahini. The first line of the song was \u201csankati raksha mama kaant\nkaant\u201d (\u201cprotect me from crisis, dear husband\u201d).<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Narayanrao completed\nhis prison sentence and was released. &nbsp;No college was willing to admit him. &nbsp;He\nwent to Calcutta and somehow secured admission in the National Medical College. &nbsp;Calcutta was far from Nasik. &nbsp;He was\nwatched all the time. In 1912, when a bomb was hurled in Delhi on Lord\nHardinge, he was arrested and brought to Pune but was released after a few\ndays. In 1916, he qualified as a doctor and married Shantabhai.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Yesuvahini led a frugal life. She had two sets of worn out clothes.. She had lost all interest in\nlife and was malnourished.&nbsp; Her health\nwas now failing. &nbsp;In 1918,&nbsp; her whole body\nwas swolled and she was bed ridden. Narayanrao and his wife Shantabai were by\nher side when her end came.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-cTV39iw9gcQ/UEToH5gpe0I/AAAAAAAAQns/p3ltMa_IM30/s1600/imagesCCDDE.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-cTV39iw9gcQ/UEToH5gpe0I/AAAAAAAAQns/p3ltMa_IM30/s1600/imagesCCDDE.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Yesuvahini had become delirious.\n. She gave one last pitiful glance at Narayanrao and passed away on 20 April 1919 . &nbsp;Three days after she died, an official letter arrived\nfrom the British, morbid mockery at its best \u201cThere is no objection to Yashodabai\nSavarkar going to the Andamans to meet her husband\u201d. This type of a foul \"cock a snook\" &nbsp;move is unthinkable in Sanatana Dharma or in any cultured society.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">From the warden to the\nclerk, most of the jail officers in the Cellular Jail were Muslims. They would\ncollude with Barrie and prove their loyalty to him by committing atrocities on\nthe prisoners. They would induce the prisoners to embrace Islam by threatening\nthem with punishment , luring them with tobacco and giving them food which was NOT laced with kerosene and human sweat..</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">On an average, two or three\nHindu prisoners would get converted in every month. &nbsp;To get food\nwithout Kerosene and wringed out sweat , converted Muslim prisoners would no\nlonger dine with their fellow Hindu prisoners but would openly dine with Muslim\nprisoners.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">One day unable to\ntolerate the continuous smell of kerosene in his food, Ganesh threw his food\naway.&nbsp; This sudden act smashed the flood gates of human emotion . Soon discontent became a full blown revolt. &nbsp;Throwing away food by prisoners was considered to be a grave offence. Prisoners\nwould be forced to eat up the last morsel of thrown food from the floor . Babarao resolutely\nrefuse to eat the food from the floor.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Babarao thus took the lead\nin this first ever mass strike at Cellular jail. Barrie singled out Nandgopal, and\nBabarao as the leaders . &nbsp;Babarao was punished on cross bar fetters and standing\nhandcuffs for a week. They were given nothing to eat for twelve days except for\nthin gruel laced with quinine...The strike went on for several days.
