In the\nend, it was Barrie and the British who had to relent--as hanging enmasse was NOT an option.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Enr5IkgBSAg/UETpw4OlkkI/AAAAAAAAQoU/bNv5hHaHodE/s1600/aaaaaa.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Enr5IkgBSAg/UETpw4OlkkI/AAAAAAAAQoU/bNv5hHaHodE/s1600/aaaaaa.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Barre agreed to stop the chakki (kolu)\npunishment, give light work and send the political prisoners outside the\nCellular Jail to do work, as was the case with other prisoners. The strike was\ncalled off. &nbsp; Babarao was spared of the\nkolu,&nbsp; and made to break dry coconuts.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-K7flHXCKOjs/UETp6r2vsdI/AAAAAAAAQoc/f4gGJcEIVLM/s1600/cvbbb.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-K7flHXCKOjs/UETp6r2vsdI/AAAAAAAAQoc/f4gGJcEIVLM/s1600/cvbbb.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Each prisoner was given to read one book at a time if he so desired. The\nprisoners were not expected to exchange books. If they did so, they were\npunished.. Before the strike only one letter to home ( and that too censored ) per year was allowed.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Babarao\u2019s younger\nbrother Vinayak Tatyarao arrived at the Cellular Jail on 04 July 1911. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Savarkar brothers\nBabarao and Vinayak didn't know of each other in the same jail but in different\ncells, for nearly two years.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The news that Tatyarao\nwas also lodged in the Cellular Jail was broken to Babarao by Wamanrao Joshi\nwho had been sentenced to Transportation for Life in the Jackson murder case.\nVinayak of course knew that his elder brother was somewhere in the jail.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Tatyarao finally\nsucceeded in meeting Babarao. The brothers had last met in 1906 when Tatyarao\nwas ready to depart from Mumbai harbour to go to England to become a\nbarrister. They were now meeting 5 years later in 1911 under totally different\ncircumstances.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-CeXd27PqJ24/UETqI9Zpw7I/AAAAAAAAQos/9gBZOmq8DKs/s1600/555.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-CeXd27PqJ24/UETqI9Zpw7I/AAAAAAAAQos/9gBZOmq8DKs/s400/555.jpg\" width=\"293\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The coronation of King\nGeorge V and Queen May (or Queen Mary as she was later called ) took place at\nWestminster Abbey on 22 June 1911. &nbsp;Later that year, the King and Queen\ntravelled to India for the Delhi Durbar on 12 December, where they were\npresented to an assembled audience of Indian dignitaries and princes as the\nEmperor and Empress of India. &nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">George wore the newly-created Imperial. Crown of\nIndia at the ceremony. He would show that he was in charge of the destiny of India. He went for a quick win.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">The King gave carrot and stick&nbsp;</span>largesse<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">. &nbsp;The British government would\nrelease all political prisoners as a goodwill gesture. &nbsp;All the prisoners were\nlined up. Barrie and the jail superintendent marched in. Each prisoner was\ncalled ceremoniously and the extent&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 24px;\">of commutation</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;of his sentence was announced. When\nBabarao\u2019s turn came, one measly month was reduced from each year of his jail sentence.\n<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">By August 1918, &nbsp;Baburao\u2019s weight had dropped down to a mere 42 kilos and he had shooting pain from his\ngall bladder. &nbsp;Towards the end of 1919, when he could no longer walk, the jail\nsuperintendent sent<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Babarao\u2019s sputum for\nexamination. The doctors diagnosed tuberculosis. &nbsp;Initially, political prisoners\nwould not be sent to hospital, they were left to die.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Due to the strike by the political prisoners, and due to orders from Britain, the\njail officials gradually started sending sick political prisoners to hospital. &nbsp;Even Vinayak Tatyarao was kept in hospital for one year when he fell ill. &nbsp;But&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Babarao was not so\nfortunate .Neither did he receive any medicines nor was he sent to hospital. Even\nwhen he had fever of 102 \u00baF, diarrhea and cough, he was made to do hard\nlabour.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Back home the youngest\nbrother, Narayanrao made earnest efforts to secure the release of his two elder\nbrothers Babarao and Tatyarao. &nbsp;Babarao\u2019s first letter from the Andamans reached\nNarayanrao in July 1912. &nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">On 24 December 1919, the Bombay Government said that\nit was willing to consider the proposal for clemency in case of all political\nprisoners except the Savarkar brothers! In a telegram dated 30 December 1919, the\nGovernment of India seconded the opinion that the Savarkar brothers be excluded\nfrom general clemency.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">In February 1920, Lokmanya Bal Gangadhara&nbsp;</span>Tilak himself<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"> wrote directly to Montague demanding that </span>Tatyarao<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"> be freed. In&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 24px;\">a memorandum</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;dated 30 March 1920, </span>Savarkar<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"> listed various reasons why </span>Babarao\nVinayak<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"> and he should be released. The Bombay Government could not care less.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">In\n1920, the National Union presented a memorandum to the government demanding\nthe release of the Savarkar brothers. The memorandum had 70000 signatures. &nbsp;In\nFebruary 1920 the Government refused to accept this petition on the flimsy\ngrounds that it was not addressed to the Cabinet Minister for India--just a sham excuse.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">In an\narticle entitled Savarkar brothers written in Young India dated 26 May 1920, Mahatma\nGandhi supported the demand for their release of the Savarkar brothers. &nbsp;Mahatma Gandhi had the power -- British would listen only to him. &nbsp; So the people of India were forced to follow Gandhiji. Gandhiji was their type of freedom fighter. He was non-violent.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">It was now well known in India that Ganesh\nBabarao Savarkar would die soon of gall bladder inflammation. Already Kanhare\nand Dhingra had shown what could happen to the British when it came to Ganesh\nSavarkar.&nbsp; .&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-XIBZ_EOA8yM/UETrkllQ58I/AAAAAAAAQpU/qz-Tt2JkSQc/s1600/imagesnnn.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-XIBZ_EOA8yM/UETrkllQ58I/AAAAAAAAQpU/qz-Tt2JkSQc/s1600/imagesnnn.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Babarao and Tatyarao were\nnow asked to pack their belongings.. There was happiness and celebrations in\nCellular jail. &nbsp;Many cried with joy, some brought flowers, others gave gifts. The\nbrothers were moved. &nbsp;In his farewell address,Tatyarao Vinayak , the lawyer from\nBritain,&nbsp; gave a message to those\npresent: \u201cEk dev, ek desh, ek aashaa, Ek jaati, ek jeev, ek bhaashaa\u201d (\u201cOne\ngod, one country, one aspiration, One community, one life, one language\u201d)</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-uyRn7-u0F-0/UETrfmYU1xI/AAAAAAAAQpM/cmpE6-ujM5w/s1600/imageskirew.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-uyRn7-u0F-0/UETrfmYU1xI/AAAAAAAAQpM/cmpE6-ujM5w/s1600/imageskirew.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">On 02\nMay 1921, the guard told them that a posse of guards had arrived to accompany\nthem to the mainland. Both Babarao and Tatyarao were made to stand near the\ngates of the Cellular Jail. They were handed over to their new guards. The guard\nsaid that it was not necessary to bind them in fetters any more. &nbsp;Babarao had entered\nthese gates in 1910, Tatyarao had followed him in 1911..</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The two brothers\nstarted walking towards the sea to board MV. Maharaja to a tearfull farewell. After a horrible sea crossing , when they saw India\u2019s coastline,\nTatyarao exclaimed to Babarao, \u201cBaba, look at Bharat mata\u201d . Both stood up and\nfolded their hands in reverence.\u201cSwatantryalakshmi ki jai Vande Mataram!! ( Salute to the Goddess of Liberty! Salute to the Motherland!!).</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">After landing in Calcutta,\nthe two brothers were kept for fifteen days in Alipore jail. &nbsp;On 26 May 1921,\nthey were separated. &nbsp;Babarao was escorted by two British guards and dragged\naway as he could not walk because of the gall bladder pain. &nbsp;Tatyarao wondered\nif this was the last time he would be seeing his brother alive.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Babarao was put in\na train.. After two days, he was in another jail.</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">. It was then that he was told\nthat this was Bijapur jail for solitary confinement. &nbsp;Two guards led Babarao\nthrough a narrow tunnel and thrown into a dark dungeon full of mosquitoes and\ninsects-- retribution for the strike he lead at the Cellular jail.&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Just when he\nwas thinking positive , that at least there is no chakki to peese , the petty warden and a couple of guards thrust a huge wheat grinder and a sack of wheat into the cell. \u201cThat is your\npunishment. If you do not grind this wheat to fine powder in another 8 hours, &nbsp;you shall receive\nfurther punishment \u201d</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">For last twelve years, &nbsp;Babarao had been subjected to the\nworst torture and he could NOT even stand . Diarrhoea, migraine, cough and\ntuberculosis were all slowly wasting away his body. &nbsp;But Babarao\u2019s spirit and pride was\nuncommon. &nbsp;He mustered his last reserves and started grinding the chakki. &nbsp;Ganesh spent another five months in\nBijapur laboring this way. &nbsp;The period from November 1921 to January 1922 was\nspent at the doorstep of death.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-SiHig0RFRgE/UETrAahv0oI/AAAAAAAAQo8/rgMJROoRgLA/s1600/hhjki.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-SiHig0RFRgE/UETrAahv0oI/AAAAAAAAQo8/rgMJROoRgLA/s1600/hhjki.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">It was in the beginning of December 1921 that\nthe youngest brother Narayanrao finally got permission to meet Babarao. When he\nwent to meet Babarao in jail&nbsp; the warden\nrudely told him, \u201cTake off your bloody &nbsp;Gandhi cap. You cannot see him that\nway.\u201d &nbsp;Infuriated by this insult, Narayanrao turned back without meeting Babarao. &nbsp;He shot off telegrams to the Viceroy, District Magistrate and to all the\nnewspapers. The Government had to relent. &nbsp;Narayanrao had his way.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">But what Narayanrao\nnow saw before him was almost a living corpse. Babarao could not speak more\nthan a minute at a time before he would become breathless and he could not look\nat the light. When Narayanrao reached Mumbai, he publicized the harrowing\ntreatment being meted out to Babarao with the assistance of Horniman of Bombay\nChronicle.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">This had the desired effect. Towards the end of January 1922, Babarao\nwas shifted out of the horrible Bijapur Jail. &nbsp;He was promptly lodged in the\nSabarmati Jail. &nbsp;Babarao had spent the period from May 1921 to January 1922 in\nBijapur Jail. These eight months of solitary confinement were even more\nterrible than the years in the Cellular Jail. &nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">On January 1922, Babarao was\nshifted to the Sabarmati Jail again in solitary confinement.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The other inmates of Sabarmati jail were\nconvinced that Babarao would not recover . The Sindhi leader Jairamdas Daulatram\nfelt that a great man like&nbsp; Babarao must\nnot die this way. &nbsp;He wrote a report on Babarao\u2019s condition with the intention\nof sending it to Narayanrao. One of prison officials kindly agreed to smuggle it out\nof prison at his own risk.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">He took the letter and went straight to the Gandhi ashram in\nSabarmati. He met a Maharashtrian Gandhian named Kakarnamak and asked him to\npost the letter from Karnavati &nbsp;(now Ahmedabad). &nbsp;This precaution was taken just\nin case the letter was found and the sender was traced.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The prison official\nexplained to Kakarnamak that a fellow Maratha , Babarao Savarkar, the great revolutionary was\ncounting his last moments in Sabarmati Jail. The letter written to his\nyounger brother would give Babarao the satisfaction of dying on his brother\u2019s\nlap.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">That \u201ctrue Gandhian\u201d replied &nbsp;, the way he was tutored , \u201cI am a follower of Gandhi and a firm\nbeliever in truth and non-violence. Doing clandestine activities is against our\nphilosophy and hence tantamount to sin. Forgive me. I shall not be able to\ncomply with your request.\u201d</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The prison official was dumb-struck and dismayed at the Gandhian\u2019s\nattitude. He turned back without a word, gave money to a total stranger and asked him\nto post the letter at Karnavati.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">At the\ntime , the national leadership had passed into the hands of Mahatma Gandhi-- and\nGandhiji did NOT want any Babarao Ganesh Savarkar around. &nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Netaji Bose would understand what I mean.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The letter reached Narayanrao. On reading its\ncontents, Narayanrao started running from pillar to post to arrange for\nBabarao\u2019s medical treatment. &nbsp;A Civil Surgeon landed in Sabarmati Jail to examine\nBabarao. The Civil Surgeon examined Babarao from 9.00 am to 2.00 pm. He opined\nthat Babarao may live for another 1-2 days at the most.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">He conveyed his opinion\nto the Administrator. Fearing that the Government would be answerable if Babarao\nwere to die within the four walls of the prison, the Administrator promptly\nissued orders for Babarao\u2019s release. He also wrote to Narayanrao, \u201cYour brother\nhas been released .Make your own arrangements to take him away from Sabarmati Jail.\u201d</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">It was\nonly after the Government was convinced that Babarao would surely die that he\nwas finally released. He was brought out of jail on a stretcher. As he was being\ntaken out, Bhansali embraced Babarao and began sobbing like a child. There was not a dry eye around.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Babarao finally emerged out of Sabarmati jail on a stretcher. He had entered jail in June 1909. It was in September 1922\nthat he was finally released . Babarao thus spent over thirteen years in prison\nunder the most harrowing conditions. But the toll was severe . This mountain of a virile yogi had become\na virtual corpse.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Babarao under brotherly\nlove and care, defied logic and death . He miraculously survived. &nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">He was&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">destined to live for\nanother twenty-three years.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The spirit of Babarao\nwas intact. The year was 1923. &nbsp;Mamarao Joglekar, the eminent Hindu leader from\nAkola (Maharashtra) was traveling from Kalyan to Nashik by train. &nbsp;Seated\nopposite to him was Professor Damodar Ganesh Padhye from Nashik. &nbsp;As the train\nhalted at a station, Padhye alighted from the train to buy some fruits. &nbsp;He kept\nhis pugree (traditional Maharashtrian headgear) and umbrella on his seat and\nleft his seat.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">As soon as he alighted, a burly Pathan shifted from his seat, threw away his belongings\nand sat there in his place. When Padhye came back, he was surprised to see the\nPathan there. Padhye pleaded with the Pathan to allow him to occupy his rightful\nplace. However, the arrogant Pathan started acting tough abusing frail Padhye.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Suddenly, a sickly frail passenger who was sitting two places away\ngot up and leaped on the Pathan. Apparently trained in wrestling he brought down the Pathan in a moment and sitting on the\nPathan\u2019s chest, started raining blows on him. &nbsp;Next, he tugged so hard at\nthe Pathan\u2019s beard that a handful of hair came off. And that snapped the Pathan back to reality.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The Pathan started howling\nin pain. Terrified, he beat a hasty retreat. Shouting \u201cTobaa, Tobaa, Ya\nAllah\u201d, the Pathan went to another compartment .</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Mamarao Joglekar who was a\nwitness to this remarkable incident asked the sickly passenger his name.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">\u201cMy\nname is Baba Ganesh Savarkar\u201d was the reply! <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">A new phase in\nBabarao\u2019s life started. &nbsp;This was the phase as thinker, writer and organizer.\nTill he died Babarao devoted himself to the task of awakening Hindu society .\nHe tried his best to close the fissures a fellow Maharashtrian , a Mahar by the name of BR Ambedkar, as a stooge of the British, &nbsp;introduced to Hindu\nsociety.. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Babarao<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"> wrote the book\n</span>Rashtramimansa va Hindusthanche rashtraswaroop<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"> in 1931 when he was in\n</span>Kashi<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">. This is widely regarded as his </span>bestwork<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">. &nbsp;He would start an freedom\nfighting&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 24px;\">organisation</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;by the name of </span>RSS<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;. &nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Babarao would design the flag of </span>RSS<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">. &nbsp;He would write the pledge for </span>RSS<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Towards the end of\n1924, Babarao arrived in Nagpur. He was put up at the residence of Advocate\nVishwanathrao Kelkar who was his distant relative and Dr. Hedgewar\u2019s close\nfriend. Babarao used to attract patriotic youngsters wherever he went. His stay in Nagpur\nsaw several youngsters visiting him and discussing the state of the sad state of India and Hindu\nsociety.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Among these youngsters was Dr. Hedgewar. Babarao became convinced that\nthere was no one more suitable than Dr. Hedgewar to carry forward the freedom\nfighting activities . Dr. Hedgewar translated his long cherished dream into\nreality on Vijayadashmi day in 1925. &nbsp;This was the beginning of the Rashtriya\nSwayamsevak Sangh (RSS).<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">RSS would counter the\npropaganda of BR Ambedkar , by deeds. &nbsp;BR Ambedkar , on behalf of the British would be shouting from the rooftops about Britsih rule being better for the lower castes than self rule.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">There was NIL casteism in RSS. &nbsp;The RSS\ncadres knew not nor cared not who was Brahmin and who was untouchable.&nbsp; They ate together and slept together. They drank water from the same tumbler.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">This was a time when\nthe British started hanging the Indian freedom fighters enmasse, for flimsy\nreasons , using traitor Muslim Indians as connivers and false witnesses. .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Mahatma Gandhi\nsaid&nbsp; \"When I visited the RSS Camp,\nI was very much surprised by your discipline and absence of\nuntouchablity.\" He personally inquired to low caste Swayamsevaks and found\nthat they were living and eating together in the camp without bothering to know\ntheir castes.&nbsp; This was Utopia .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Even a high strung\ncharacter like BR Ambedkar, who could NOT see outside the Dalit prism, admitted \" This is the first time that I am visiting the camp of Sangh volunters. I\nam happy to find absolute equality between Savarniyas (Upper cast) and Harijans\n(Lower cast) without any one being aware of such difference existing. When I\nasked asked Dr Hedgewar whether there were any untouchables in the camp, he\nreplied that there are neither \"touchables\" nor\n\"untouchables\" but only Hindus.\u201d.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">BR Ambedkar and Mahatma\nGandhi knew in their hearts, that their Harijan uplift theory was only on\npaper, and only RSS had the means and power to convert it into practise. Since when\nhas deeds become less important than words? &nbsp;&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Babarao often wondered why Gandhiji placed Sanskrit after Arabic,\nPersian and Urdu in order of importance. He felt sad at the way Gandhiji appeased the Muslims and had underhand dealings with the British.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">BR Ambedkar who was\ngroomed by Winston Churchill to drive a wedge into the heart of Hinduism, was sent for Higher education to Opium drug funded Columbia University, owned by British East India Company. &nbsp;He was ironically given Bharat\nRatna. &nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">BR Ambedkar did NOT want British to leave India.&nbsp; He did NOT spend a single minute of his life\nin any freedom struggle.&nbsp; I dare anybody\nto prove me wrong. When the entire nation had risen against the British in\n1857, only the Mahar caste of BR Ambedkar, has supported the British, along with the Sikhs. Rest everbody including Muslims fought against Britain.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Gandhi\u2019s treachery against the\nrevolutionaries and Gandhi\u2019s efforts to crown the rabid Islamic Nizam as the\nsovereign of a future sovereign Hindusthan, &nbsp;and the appeasement policies pursued\nby the Congress deeply pained Babarao.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">In 1924-25, </span>Babarao<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"> was\nin </span>Dhantoli<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"> (Nagpur) to recuperate from illness. There, he met a scholar from\n</span>Andhra Pradesh<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"> who had a treasure of information on Jesus </span>from old<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"> Sanskrit\narchives.&nbsp; The scholar mentioned to </span>Babarao<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nthat </span>Ramaswamy Iyer<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">, a resident of Madras (now Chennai) had done some research which proved that Jesus was a &nbsp;Hindu. &nbsp;It is a well known fact that Jesus\nwas in </span>Kerala<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"> for three years learning Ayurveda,&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 24px;\">mediation</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;and healing , before he burst upon the scene at Jerusalem&nbsp;</span>suddenly&nbsp;as a full grown adult<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">As evidence to show\nthat Christ came to Hindusthan, &nbsp;Babarao mentions books such as\nNaatha-Naamaavali, Tarikh-i-Ajam, Ikmaba Udadinan d Barlan the Josephet. &nbsp;Babarao too concluded that Jesus was a Hindu.. He exhorted&nbsp; the Christians in Hindusthan to accept the\nfact that they are not different from the Hindus but members of a cult\nestablished by a Hindu philosopher , like Buddha..<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Babarao\u2019s well-wishers\nwould then warn him that he would lose popularity and be shunned by the people\nat large and Congressmen in particular if he continued to criticize Gandhi. Babarao\nwould calmly reply that he had forsaken his home ,hearth and wife for the sake\nof his motherland. &nbsp;He would continue to expose Gandhi\u2019s anti- Hindu activities, and the truth, even\nif that meant inviting contempt and ridicule.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">On 14 March, 1945, he\nlost the ability to speak. He could barely breathe. His whole body was\nswollen. When he was shifted from his sickbed, hundreds of red ants were found on the mattress. The attending doctors gave up hope. &nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">On 16 March, Babarao\u2019s sense of\npain vanished. .</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">He passes away at around 2.15 pm. &nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Thousands&nbsp;\nof people started pouring from different villages and towns. &nbsp;A massive\nfuneral procession started and lakhs of people including Muslims and Christians , showered flowers at different places. The\nBhagwa flag of the Rashtriya Swayamsevak Sangh was lowered at half-mast and the\nSangh prayer was sung.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Then Dr. Narayanrao\nSavarkar lit the pyre and the flames engulfed Babarao\u2019s lifeless body. Keeping\nthe funeral pyre as witness, thousands of Indians vowed to carry on the sacred\nlife mission of Babarao -- </span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: magenta;\">\u2018maa phaleshu kadaachana\u2019 ( expect not the fruit -- the Bhagwad Gita ).</span><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Back in London--&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red;\"><br /></span></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">On 17th Aug 1909, a\nChristian preacher named Hudson walked up to Dhinghra to say a final Christian\nprayer for him. &nbsp; But Dhingra turned him away saying that he was a Hindu. &nbsp;The\nDeputy Under-Sheriff of London Metcalf read out the death warrant to Dhingra in\nthe presence of Deputy Governor Hales of Pentonville prison and asked him the\nusual questions.&nbsp;</span></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-TsJRsmlHT4w/UETn13_TKcI/AAAAAAAAQnk/PXPvRX4d4MM/s1600/NGT.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-TsJRsmlHT4w/UETn13_TKcI/AAAAAAAAQnk/PXPvRX4d4MM/s1600/NGT.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">But Dhingra ignored their questions and walked calmly to the\nnoose. His bravery left the accompanying offcers dumb-founded. Officer\nPierpoint stood at the hangman's noose waiting for Dhingra. Dhingra smiled at\nhim and ascended the steps to the platform. He himself placed the noose round\nhis neck.&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red;\"><br /></span></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">Soon thereafter, the wooden platform underneath was withdrawn.\nDhingra's body dropped eight feet and lay hanging. As per convention, his limp\nbody was left hanging for half an hour. When his body was brought down, the\nface was smiling.&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">He had avenged the illegal deportation to Kaala pani, of a great Indian\npatriot by the name of Ganesh Babarao Savarkar.&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red;\"><br /></span></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">Dhingra wished that last rites\naccording to Hindu Dharma should be performed on his dead body and it should be\ncremated. &nbsp;Many Hindus petitioned to the Home Secretary Mr Herbert Gladstone\nthat Dhingra's body should be handed over to them, as several Brahmins were ready to\nperform the last rites.&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">This request was denied! &nbsp;The last wish of a man sent to\nthe gallows was denied--such was British justice! &nbsp;His body was put in a coffin, which was buried within\nthe prison premises.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">After Dhingra went to the gallows, the Times, London wrote\nan editorial (24 July 1909) titled 'Conviction of Dhingra\". &nbsp;The editorial\nsaid, \"The nonchalance displayed by the assassin was of a character, which\nis happily unusual in such trials in this country. He asked no questions. He\nmaintained a defiance of studied indifference. He walked smiling from the\nDock.\"<o:p></o:p></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Iqfwc5Ki9Fc/UETouCzrxuI/AAAAAAAAQn8/Vs7UzCZNbic/s1600/imagesBGYYYY.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Iqfwc5Ki9Fc/UETouCzrxuI/AAAAAAAAQn8/Vs7UzCZNbic/s400/imagesBGYYYY.jpg\" width=\"348\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Madanlal Dhingra\u2019s\nfinal statement was as inspiring as his actions. Titled \u2018Challenge\u2019 it read as\nfollows:<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Challenge<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">1. \"I admit the\nother day; I attempted to shed English blood as an humble revenge for the\ninhuman hangings and deportations of patriotic Indian youths. In this attempt,\nI have consulted none but my own conscience; I have conspired with none, but my\nown duty.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">2. \"I believe that\na nation held down in bondage with the help of foreign bayonets is in a\nperpetual state of war. Since open battle is rendered impossible to a disarmed\nrace, I attacked by surprise; since guns were denied to me, I drew forth my\npistol and fired.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">3. \"As a Hindu I\nfelt that a wrong done to my country is an insult to God. Her cause is the\ncause of Sri Ram! Her services are the services of Sri Krishna! Poor in health\nand intellect, a son like myself has nothing else to offer to the Mother but\nhis own blood and so I have sacrificed the same on her altar.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">4. \"The only\nlesson required in India at present is to learn how to die and the only way to\nteach it, is by dying ourselves. Therefore I die and glory in my martyrdom!\nThis war of Independence will continue between India and England, so long as\nthe Hindu and the English races last (if the present unnatural relation does\nnot cease!)<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">5. \"My only prayer\nto God is: May I be reborn of the same Mother and may I redie in the same sacred\ncause, till the cause is successful and she stands free for the good of\nhumanity and the glory of God!\"<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;-Vande Mataram-<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Dhingra's martyrdom\nevoked the respect of some members of the Cabinet. This was disclosed later to\nBlunt by Winston Churchill. Blunt writes (My Diaries, Vol.2, p. 288, entry for\n03 October 1909),&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red;\"><br /></span></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">\"Again we sat up late. Among the many memorable things\nChurchill said was this. Talking of Dhingra, he said that there has been much\ndiscussion in the Cabinet about him. Lloyd George had expressed to him his\nhighest admiration of Dhingra's attitude as a patriot, in which he shared\u2026\" <i>He\nwill be remembered two thousand years hence, as we remember Regulus and\nCaractacus and Plutarch's heroes and Churchill quoted with admiration Dhingra's\nlast words, as the finest, ever made in the name of patriotism</i>\u2026\"<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">\u201cI do not care for my\nlife. You are all powerful. You can do what you like. &nbsp; But remember, that one\nday India shall be powerful and then we shall do what we like\" were his last\nwords when the English judge read his sentence.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">During his brief stay\nin London, <span style=\"background-color: yellow;\">Gandhi, the much-touted apostle of non violence, deplored Madanlal\nDhingra and other revolutionaries to please the British, declared them\nanarchists</span> and said, \u201cIs killing honourable? &nbsp;Is the dagger of an assassin a fit\nprecursor of an honourable death?\u201d<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Dhingra\u2019s martyrdom and\nhis last statement evoked widespread sympathy and admiration in Ireland. &nbsp;Posters entitled \u201cIreland Honours Dhingra\u201d along with the last statement\nadorned the walls in Ireland.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Madan Lal Dhingra's<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\ncoffin was exhumed on 12 December 1976 in the presence of </span>Natwar<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"> Singh, then\nActing High&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 24px;\">Commissioner</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;for India and the coffin flown back to India.&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: red;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"color: red;\">Madan Lal Dhingra<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"> lives on in the hearts of his country men.&nbsp;</span></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: red;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span>\n</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Now, some doodh ka doodh paani ka paani--</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />The cry&nbsp;<span style=\"color: blue;\">JAI HIND&nbsp;</span>was NOT coined by Netaji Bose. &nbsp;It was made by&nbsp;<span style=\"line-height: 36px;\">Dr Champakaraman Pillai ,&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 36px;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 36px;\">who formed the Berlin Committee in Germany to assist freedom fighters before the 1</span><sup style=\"line-height: 30px;\">st</sup><span style=\"line-height: 36px;\">&nbsp;World war . He &nbsp;had direct dealings with Hitler. He died on May 28th, 1934 under suspicious circumstances , because he asked for a written apology from Hitler with a deadline, for derogatory reference to Indians in his book Mein Kamph.. His ashes were scattered in Karamana River in Thiruvananthapuram. &nbsp;His ashes could not be brought in before, due to objections from Gandhiji and Nehru . The Indian Navy's warship, I.N.S. Delhi, flying the flag of Free India, brought the great patriot Pillai's ashes to Cochin on September 16, 1966.&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 36px;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 36px;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 36px;\">He had come to Madras on German battleship, SS Emden and&nbsp;</span><i style=\"line-height: 36px;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">angrez ka ghar mein ghuske maara</span></i><span style=\"line-height: 36px;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">.</span>&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 36px;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Punch into Google\nsearch-</span></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><b style=\"background-color: yellow;\">AN OFFICER AND A\nGENTLEMEN, KARL VON MULLER , CAPTAIN OF SMS EMDEN VADAKAYIL</b><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; His ashes too were rejected by Gandhi and Nehru. &nbsp;Finally Bollywood actor Vinod Khanna , Narendra Modi , and others etc pulled levers, and this great patriot's ashes was officially handed over to the Chief Minister of Gujarat State on August 22, 2003, &nbsp;by the Ville de Gen\u00e8ve and the Swiss government, 55 years after Indian Independence.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />Well what do we know?-- the young generation knows Diggi Vijay , Ambika Soni , Anand Sharma , Kapil Sibal etc , right?</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: small;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span></span>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: magenta; font-size: x-large;\"><b>ARE THERE ARE MORE OF SUCH&nbsp;</b></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: magenta; font-size: x-large;\"><b><br /></b></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><b><span style=\"color: magenta; font-size: x-large;\">PATRIOTS IN INDIA? Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "6", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/740679316577706244/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "564526998200252640", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2012-08-30T11:36:00+05:30", "updated": "2012-09-16T22:24:25+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxMzQ3ODE0NDY1OTA4Cm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2012/08/truck-art-of-pakistan-capt-ajit.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/564526998200252640", "title": "TRUCK ART OF PAKISTAN - CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\">\n<span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\"><b>TRUCK ART OF PAKISTAN, AND MAHIRA KHAN&nbsp;</b></span>- CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL<br />\n<br />\nTwo decades ago I was working for an American owner. He had a GM Operations ( a Sikh ) who took lot of sadistic pleasure ( in the email era ) to put as many abbreviations as possible in the long voyage orders.<br />\n<br />\nAnd to make things worse , he used to omit AEIOU vowels . &nbsp;This was all right in the morse code era, to keep radio officer on his toes and to save money . &nbsp;But in the email era you&nbsp;don't&nbsp;save any money and if you do that you are a dork. &nbsp;Young masters used to go into a tizzy when they received such a message from the GM, as they did NOT want to appear incompetent.<br />\n<br />\nPunch into Google search ABBREVIATIONS ON CHEMICAL TANKERS- VADAKAYIL, where I put a small percentage of it.<br />\n<br />\nSo once when I replied I put <span style=\"color: blue;\">PYTNK </span>under my signature.<br />\n<br />\nSo one day curiosity overtook the Sardarjee and he asked me, Captain could you please tell me what is PVTNK.<br />\n<br />\nSo I replied \" Yaar, I have given you a abbreviation from your neck of the woods. I have seen Punjabi trucks having logos like:<br />\n<br />\nSOUND HORN OK<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: blue;\">PAPPU YAAR TANGH NA KAR ( &nbsp;Pappu buddy, dont &nbsp;fu#k around with me )</span><br />\n<br />\nBUREE NAZAR WAALE TERA MOONH KAALA &nbsp;.( Ye with evil eyes, here is some black soot for your fu#kin' face )<br />\n<br />\nIn Pakistan I have seen several more hilarious ones-- rather more profound ones , like:--<br />\n<br />\nDEKH MAGAR PYAR SE &nbsp;( ye may look, but only with love )<br />\n<br />\nMEHNAT KAR HASSAD NA KAR ( work ,&nbsp;don't&nbsp;be jealous )<br />\n<br />\nMA KI DUA JANNAT KE HAWA ( blessings from mother, is like&nbsp;breeze&nbsp;from heaven )<br />\n<br />\netc etc<br />\n<br />\nWhen I went to Pakistan nearly 4 decades ago, the truck which I saw were all garishly decorated with \"Truck art\"-- literally a&nbsp;cacophony&nbsp;of&nbsp;colors. It jarred your senses.<br />\n<br />\nCalligraphy was hard to understand. They had corny graffitti, like \" My truck is my space ship and I am its lone occupant \". &nbsp;The art was basically hallucinating escapism from harsh reality.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-T38P9W1VJes/UD8CGWG8rtI/AAAAAAAAQWA/rZghBO7Tm_8/s1600/imagesxxx.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"274\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-T38P9W1VJes/UD8CGWG8rtI/AAAAAAAAQWA/rZghBO7Tm_8/s400/imagesxxx.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nA few months ago when my ship went to Karachi, I noted the marked change in truck art. &nbsp;It was almost like mehndi art on the hands of a Indian bride. <br />\n<br />\nI have a tattoo myself. &nbsp;I love mE stupid &nbsp;tattoo, and I&nbsp;don't&nbsp;care if anybody else appreciates it or not. &nbsp;For me it is about a feel good factor.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-o0zub_TxxA8/UD8BUBQd1bI/AAAAAAAAQVg/qZykF43AF_4/s1600/truck-art-pakistan-5.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-o0zub_TxxA8/UD8BUBQd1bI/AAAAAAAAQVg/qZykF43AF_4/s400/truck-art-pakistan-5.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\nTruck&nbsp;art of Pakistan is like personal tattoos. The only difference is that it is on a truck. It is MENTAL FINGER PRINTING or <i>mann ka tamanna. &nbsp;</i><br />\n<br />\nDreams and hopes , instead of aesthetic culture is what i can see--as a man who can read the subconscious.. And if the art can catch the glad eye of a pretty lass on the road, why not?<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-BEcJWOt4kEA/UD8Byw1PKbI/AAAAAAAAQV4/fMzA3fIe-nM/s1600/decorative-pakistan-truck-art-9.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"300\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-BEcJWOt4kEA/UD8Byw1PKbI/AAAAAAAAQV4/fMzA3fIe-nM/s400/decorative-pakistan-truck-art-9.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThe art is talismanic too, probably warding off evil. &nbsp; Flowers, exotic animals, hawkish birds, fighter jets, defiant clenched arms with barbed wire around the beeling wrists, waterfalls, Umrao Jaan type bejewelled mujra girls with pouting red lips, local warlords with AK47s, --<br />\n<br />\n-- among other delightful trinkets--<br />\n<br />\n- all find space among tiny mirror mosaic glinting in the sun or sweeping headlights , plus swinging chains on the bumper, which kiss the road while sashaying.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-gBpzbwLtN1s/UD8BbvIOJ_I/AAAAAAAAQVo/MVSiNAaXcr0/s1600/imagessssw.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"317\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-gBpzbwLtN1s/UD8BbvIOJ_I/AAAAAAAAQVo/MVSiNAaXcr0/s400/imagessssw.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThe driver, takes pride in the art. The owner of a new&nbsp;truck&nbsp;will spend a lot of money to&nbsp;customize&nbsp;the truck with truck art. Most of the time he will let the driver, choose what he wants, to develop a sense of belonging.<br />\n<br />\nFor the owner it makes sense if the truck driver is in platonic love with his truck. The truck art will give a general idea which Pakistani district it is from. So at a roadside Dhaba ( restaurant ) it is easy to bond with another truck driver.<br />\n<br />\nOn top of the drivers cabin, a huge helipad type deck is made , for the truck driver and cleaner to sleep, watching the stars , with the breeze blowing past-- in total privacy.<br />\n<br />\nThey could even smuggle a bonny lass on top for a tete e tete , without fear of peeping toms and prying eyes. &nbsp;It is so easy to get into \"breaking news\" nowadays.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-iOUM9Rh9LNs/UD8Bij8FCYI/AAAAAAAAQVw/kY-ZR6hiV0Q/s1600/tr_5.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"295\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-iOUM9Rh9LNs/UD8Bij8FCYI/AAAAAAAAQVw/kY-ZR6hiV0Q/s400/tr_5.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nConsidering most truck drivers spend more time in the truck than at home, it makes good sense. And of course it is all extra storage space, at the truck drivers disposal, in case he wants to do some private business of his own, without broken stowage.<br />\n<br />\nThe art is highly labour intensive and expensive. I saw a Pakistani movie BOL, where the hermaphrodite brother Saifi of the unmarried sisters , tried his hand at truck art to earn some money , and then all hell broke loose.<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; If there are too many proteins within the interstitial\nspaces, fluid will start to accumulate, causing edema. The lymph system\u2019s role\nof removing proteins is vital to keeping edema down.
