It is a unique festival-- the No 1 festival of Kerala-- at harvest time.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-eXRUve2aq0Y/UD32g9xouyI/AAAAAAAAQOg/h6TEllyuQOU/s1600/onam+2012.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-eXRUve2aq0Y/UD32g9xouyI/AAAAAAAAQOg/h6TEllyuQOU/s400/onam+2012.JPG\" height=\"251\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nAbove: This is the flower carpet ( pookalam ) &nbsp;in my home this year! &nbsp;This creation of fresh flowers &nbsp;is done by the whole family, &nbsp;and it indicates family dynamics.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Oimy-MX2Q34/UD32wES9NQI/AAAAAAAAQOo/5zKqUjT2Kwc/s1600/imagesnnggt.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Oimy-MX2Q34/UD32wES9NQI/AAAAAAAAQOo/5zKqUjT2Kwc/s400/imagesnnggt.jpg\" height=\"257\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nCompetitions are held all over Kerala--and the carpet could get so grand! &nbsp;It is a 10 day harvest festival-- nay-- carnival, with the grand finale on the last day Thiruonam.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-ELsYCKwS95Q/UD32_HWU2-I/AAAAAAAAQOw/tgHm2cNjnOU/s1600/imagesnngrr.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-ELsYCKwS95Q/UD32_HWU2-I/AAAAAAAAQOw/tgHm2cNjnOU/s400/imagesnngrr.jpg\" height=\"265\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nToday is the day, we feast ( Onasadhya ) and wear new clothes. &nbsp;The green thing is a banana plant leaf.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/--2ayq1Ul5Ts/UD33Mfqs_6I/AAAAAAAAQO4/JUGy-OXmFIA/s1600/imagesbnn.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/--2ayq1Ul5Ts/UD33Mfqs_6I/AAAAAAAAQO4/JUGy-OXmFIA/s400/imagesbnn.jpg\" height=\"228\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nIf any Malayali does NOT know this poem, he is a pseudo Malayali. &nbsp; It praises Asura King Mahabali who ruled Kerala. &nbsp;The people adored him. &nbsp;The gods felt jealous.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-OM9x1As6dvA/UD33tBjQowI/AAAAAAAAQPA/90VHfHccN0o/s1600/imagesbvff.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-OM9x1As6dvA/UD33tBjQowI/AAAAAAAAQPA/90VHfHccN0o/s320/imagesbvff.jpg\" height=\"320\" width=\"238\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nLord Vishnu came in Vamana ( midget brahmin ) avatar and drove him into the ground. &nbsp;He just asked for 3 paces of land. The king could give only two, and since he respected his grant, told Vishnu to place his last step on his head.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-NKbFly_4hns/UD34GO2noqI/AAAAAAAAQPI/pC1XjtWlV5w/s1600/imagesbbreer.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-NKbFly_4hns/UD34GO2noqI/AAAAAAAAQPI/pC1XjtWlV5w/s400/imagesbbreer.jpg\" height=\"400\" width=\"301\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\nLord Vishnu took on his mighty form,and with two steps crossed over the cosmos. He drove King Mahabali into the ground with his third step.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Rm0qa7egaSc/UD34TZh304I/AAAAAAAAQPQ/OP2ljRoelKI/s1600/imagesvdtyy.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Rm0qa7egaSc/UD34TZh304I/AAAAAAAAQPQ/OP2ljRoelKI/s1600/imagesvdtyy.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nVamana avatar was the 5th avatar of Vishnu, after Narasimha and before Parashurama.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-6-H_YUYgMS8/UD34sNbK-II/AAAAAAAAQPY/x9eKDBdP_8s/s1600/imagesbbnhh.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-6-H_YUYgMS8/UD34sNbK-II/AAAAAAAAQPY/x9eKDBdP_8s/s320/imagesbbnhh.jpg\" height=\"226\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nOn Onam day we welcome King Mahabali, the flower carpet if for him to sit on-- every house has it. People visit temples .<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-5AG1myROT1E/UD38zi_Ma2I/AAAAAAAAQQo/MCL8DF5wfMc/s1600/nnnn.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em;
